পেপসিন/ট্রিপসিন → আমিষ পরিপাককারী&nbsp;এনজাইম;<br>
লাইপেজ → লিপিড পরিপাককারী&nbsp;এনজাইম।<br>

                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: আলফা কোষ → গ্লুকাগন<br>

ডেল্টা কোষ → সোমাটোস্টাটিন<br>
পিপি কোষ → প্যানক্রিয়েটিক পলিপেপটাইড।<br>
[গাজী আজমল স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-১৬০]</p>

border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 3.402em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">M</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">g</mi><msub><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">O</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">H</mi></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">M</mi><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">g</mi><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>2</mn><mo>+</mo></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">O</mi><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">H</mi><mo>−</mo></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mo>∴</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">K</mi><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mi mathvariant="normal">s</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>4</mn><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi><mn>3</mn></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>4</mn><mo>×</mo><msup><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>10</mn></mrow><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>−</mo><mn>3</mn></mrow></msup></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-21">\rm Mg\left(OH\right)_2\rightarrow Mg^{2+}+2(OH^-) \\
\therefore K_{sp}=4S^3=4\times{10}^{-3} </script></span><br>
বা <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-22-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>S</mi><mo>=</mo><msup><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mn>10</mn></mrow><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-344" style="width: 3.895em;                                     <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: এখানে, <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-33-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi>l</mi></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-474" style="width: 0.33em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.248em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.15em, 1000.21em, 2.092em, -999.998em); top: -1.965em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-475"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-476" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">l</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.969em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.048em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.953em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>l</mi></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-33">l</script></span>&nbsp;এর মান হবে 0 থেকে (n-1) পর্যন্ত এবং m&nbsp;এর মান হবে শূন্যসহ <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-34-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo><mi>l</mi></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-477" style="width: 1.109em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.904em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.191em, 1000.86em, 2.215em, -999.998em); top: -2.006em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-478"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-479" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">−</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-480" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">l</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.01em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.148em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.052em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo>−</mo><mi>l</mi></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-34">-l</script></span>&nbsp;থেকে <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;                                 <div class="col-md-12" style="padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px;">
                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial">
                                            <span>Question 38 </span>
                                        </div>

width: 0px; height: 6.314em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -5.598em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 6.553em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mn>5</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">f</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mn>5</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>3</mn></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>8</mn><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mn>6</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mn>6</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>7</mn><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mn>7</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">s</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mn>7</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>7</mn><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mn>4</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mn>4</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>2</mn></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>6</mn></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-56">\rm 5f=\left(5+3\right)=8 \\ 6p=\left(6+1\right)=7 \\ 7s=\left(7+0\right)=7 \\ 4d=\left(4+2\right)=6 </script></span><br>
যেহেতু 4d অরবিটালের জন্য <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-57-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>(</mo><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>n</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>l</mi><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>)</mo></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-852" style="width: 2.83em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.297em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.15em, 1002.22em, 2.379em, -999.998em); top: -2.006em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-853"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-854" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-855" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">n</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-856" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">+</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-857" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">l</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-858" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.01em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.348em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.302em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">n</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">l</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-57">\rm (n+l)</script></span> এর মান সবচেয়ে কম তাই এটির শক্তি সবচেয়ে কম।<br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-১২৪]</p>

position: relative; width: 2.338em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.24em, 1000.95em, 4.182em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1219"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1220"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1221" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">10</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.424em; left: 0.986em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1222"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1223"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1224" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">−</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1225" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">11</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 5.166em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -4.098em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 5.152em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">a</mi><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">F</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">⇌</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">a</mi><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>2</mn><mo>+</mo></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><mn>2</mn><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">F</mi><mo>−</mo></msup><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mo>∴</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">K</mi><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mi mathvariant="normal">s</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">p</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><msup><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi><mo>×</mo><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow></mrow><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>4</mn><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi><mn>3</mn></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>4</mn><msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mn>2</mn><mo>×</mo><msup><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>10</mn></mrow><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>−</mo><mn>4</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow><mn>3</mn></msup><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mo>=</mo><mn>3.2</mn><mo>×</mo><msup><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>10</mn></mrow><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>−</mo><mn>11</mn></mrow></msup></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-82">\rm CaF_2⇌ Ca^{2+}+2F^- \\
\therefore K_{sp}={S\times\left(2S\right)}^2=4S^3=4\left(2\times{10}^{-4}\right)^3 \\
=3.2\times{10}^{-11} </script></span><br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ- ২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-২৩৯]</p>
</span>
                                    </div>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: ভরবেগ ও বলের ঘাতের মাত্রা সমীকরণ <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;                                         <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>যে বল সৃষ্টির জন্য দুটি বস্তুর প্রত্যক্ষ সংস্পর্শ প্রয়োজন তাকে স্পর্শ বল বলে। যেমন: ঘর্ষণ বল, সংঘর্ষের ফলে সৃষ্ট বল, টানা বল।<br>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>'man' এর পূর্বে বসে man (noun) কে modify করায় right এই বাক্যে adjective।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
